 alag-alag vetan sanrachanaayen asainya (civilayan), raksha carmikon or sainya nursing seva ke liye taiyaar kii gai hai
 The principles and logic behind these structures are the same
 2
 All present levels have been incorporated into the new structure
 koi nayaa str shuru nahin kiya gaya he or na hi kisi str ko hataaya gaya he
 An index of streamlining has been approved to fix minimum pay at every level of the pay structure, which depends on increasing role, responsibility and accountability at every step in the seniority order
 3
 The minimum salary has been increased from Rs 7000 to Rs 18000 per month
 nunatam str par kisi bhi navaniyukt karmchaaree kaa shuruaati vetan ab 18000 rupee hoga, jabaki navaniyukt ‘class I’ adhikari kaa shuruaati vetan 56100 rupee hoga
 This is 1: 3
 12 ke sankuchan anupaat ko darshata he, jisase yah pataa chalata he ki sidhi bhartee vaale kisi bhi ‘class I’ adhikari kaa vetan nunatam str par navaniyukt karmchaaree ke vetan se teen guna adhik hoga
 4
 vetan evam pension main sanshodhan ke uddeshy se 2
 The fitment factor of 57 will be applicable to all levels included in the pay structures
 prachlit dar par die ko shaamil karne ke baad sabhi sarkari karmchaariyon / pensionbhogiyon ke vetan / pension main 1 janvari, 2016 ko kam se kam 14
 There will be an increase of 29 percent
 5
 The rate of increment has been retained at 3 percent
 ucch mul vetan kii badaulat karmchaaree bhavishya main labhanvit honge, kyonki bhavishya main unke vetan main jo vaarshik vruddhi hogi vah vartmaan ke mukaable 2
 Would be 57 times more
 6
 The Cabinet has increased the Streamlining Index to Level 13A (brig) and Level 12A (lay
 karnal), 13 (karnal) or 13e (brigadier) main atirikt str (stage) sunishchit karke raksha sambandhi vetan sanrachana ko or behatar kar diya he, taaki sambandhit staron ke adhiktam paaydaan par sanyukt sashastr police bal (siepief) ke samakakshon ke saath samta laai ja sake
 7
 raksha or sanyukt sashastr police bal (siepief) carmikon samet vibhinn karmchaariyon par asar daalane vaale kuch anya nirnay bhi liye gaye hai, jinamein nimnlikhit shaamil hai
 • Gratuity limit has been increased from Rs 10 lakh to Rs 20 lakh
 jab bhi die 50 pratishat bad jayega tab gracuty kii seemaa 25 pratishat bad jaaegi
 • a general arrangement has been made for the payment of lump sum compensation for civil and defense personnel, which will be payable to their families and under this, the current rates will be increased from Rs 10-20 lakhs to Rs 25-45 lakhs for different categories
 has given
 • raksha balon ke karmiyon kii vibhinn shreniyon ke liye sainya seva vetan kii daren 1000, 2000, 4200 evam 6000 rupee se sanshodhit karke kramash: 3600, 5200, 10800 evam 15500 rupee kar di gai hai
 8
 cabinet ne awaas nirmaan se judi agrim raashi ko 7
 The Commission's recommendation to increase from Rs 50 lakh to Rs 25 lakh has also been approved
 karmchaariyon ko koi dikkat na ho, yah sunishchit karne ke liye 4 byaaj mukt agrimon ko barkaraar rakhaa gaya he, jinamein chikitsa ilaaj ke liye agrim, tour / sthanantaran ke liye tie, mritak karmchaariyon ke parivaar ke liye tie or altisi shaamil hai
 All other interest free advances have been discontinued
 9
 The Cabinet has also decided not to accept the recommendation to drastically increase the monthly contribution to the Central Government Employees Group Insurance Scheme (CGEGIS), as recommended by the Commission

 Apart from this, an additional burden of Rs 12,133 crore will have to be incurred for payment of arrears related to salary and pension for two months of the year 2015-16

 2 for the purpose of amendment of salary and pension

 29 pratishat kii badhat darj ho jaaegi
 5
 vetan vruddhi kii dar ko 3 pratishat par barkaraar rakhaa gaya he
 Employees will be benefited in future due to higher basic salary, because the annual increase in their salary in future will be 2 as compared to present
 57 guna zyada hogi
 6
 cabinet ne str 13e (brigadier) ke liye suvyavasthikaran suchakank main vruddhi kar or str 12e (le
 Colonel), 13 (colonel) and 13A (brigadier) have further improved the Defense related pay structure by ensuring additional levels, so that parity with Joint Armed Police Forces (CAPF) counterparts at the highest rung of the respective levels
 Can be brought 7
 Certain other decisions have also been taken to affect various employees, including Defense and Joint Armed Police Forces (CAPF) personnel, including the following
 • gracuty kii seemaa 10 lakh rupee se badhaakar 20 lakh rupee kar di gai he
 Whenever DA is increased by 50 percent, the limit of gratuity will increase by 25 percent
 • asainya evam raksha carmikon ke liye anugrah raashi ekamusth muaavje ke bhugtan hetu ek aam vyavastha kii gai he, jo unke parijanon ko dey hoga or iske tahat vartmaan daron ko vibhinn shreniyon ke liye 10-20 lakh rupee se badhaakar 25-45 lakh rupee kar diya gaya he
 • For various categories of personnel of the defense forces, the rates of military service pay have been revised from Rs 1000, 2000, 4200 and 6000 to Rs 3600, 5200, 10800 and 15500 respectively
 8
 The cabinet gave the advance amount related to housing construction
7
 50 lakh rupee se badhaakar 25 lakh rupee karne sambandhi ayog kii sifarish ko bhi manjuuri de di he
 4 interest free advances have been retained to ensure that employees do not face any problems, including advances for medical treatment, TA for tour / transfer, TA for the family of deceased employees and LTC
 anya sabhi byaaj mukt agrimon ko samaapt kar diya gaya he

 cabinet ne centre sarkaar karmchaaree samooh beemaa yojana (sijiijiies) main kiye jane vaale masik anshdaan main baari vruddhi karne kii sifarish ko bhi na maanane kaa nirnay liya he, jaisi ki ayog ne sifarish kii thi

 Earlier, six Kannada-language writers returned the award of the Kannada Sahitya Akademi for their failure to arrest the accused in the murder of senior Kannada writer Kalaburgi in Karnataka
 viranna madivalarti satish jaavare gaudaasangamesh menasikhanihanumant haaligerishridevi ve alurchidanand Mohammed Tughlaq was a king living in characteristic contradiction, which historians termed as a comment for his craze
 jisane apni sanak ke kaaran rajdhani badali or taanbe ke sikke kaa mulya chaandi ke sikke ke baraabar kar diya
 But the Tughlaq surrounded by fanatical religious walls around it was something else
 usne mazahab se pare insaan kii talash kii thi
 Both Hindus and Muslims viewed him as one
 tatkaaleen maansikta ne tughlak kii is manyata ko asweekaar kar diya or yahi ‘asweekaar’ tughlak ke sir par sanakon kaa bhoot banakar savaar ho gaya
 Girish Karnad's plot of his famous drama 'tughlaq' is not limited to the merits and demerits of Tughlaq
 isamen us samay kii paristhitiyon or tajjanit bhaawanaaon ko bhi abhivyakt kiya gaya he, jinke kaaran us samay ke aadmi kaa chintan bouna ho gaya tha or mazahab tathaa siyasat ke takaraav main harek keval apana ullu sidhaa karnaa chahta he
 Born in Maharashtra, Girish Karnad was a well-known and influential writer, artist and director
 unki maatrubhaasha kannada thi
 He went to Oxford as a 'hounds Scholar', succeeding the highest mathematics examination
 1963 main oxford uniwarsity press, madras main naukari kii par 1970 main ‘bhashaa fellowship’ paakar naukari se tyaag-patr de diya, yaheen se unke swatantra lekhan kii shuruyaat hui

 Before swearing in as Prime Minister on 22 May 2014, Narendra Modi had said that the CAG report should not be used to counter political charges
 ye jo report hoti he wo sudhaar ke sujhaavon ke liye hoti he

 anand sharma ne kaha ki vitt mantri kaa bhi sieji ke raajnneetik istemaal na karne par ek bayaan he

 vakt kya kya khel dikhaata he

 ek din swami ji atal bihari vaajapeyi kii bhi copy check karne lagenge

 Union Home Secretary Rajiv Maharishi said that there was no need to use these photographs

 grih sachiv ne is maamle par seemaa suraksha bal (biguef) se bhi safai maangi he
 Actually, BSF only provides pictures of india-pakistan border

 Information about these floodlights from the Ministry was given in the Annual Report 2016-17
 lekin seemaa par flud lits kii jaankaree dene ke liye jin tasveeron kaa istemaal kiya ve spain-morocco seemaa kii hai
 The comments mantralay kii kirkari isliye bhi hui kyonki, jis tasviir ko bharat-pakistan seemaa bataaya gaya he, vah photo 2006 main spanish photographer jevier morayano dwaara lee thi
 The picture was taken showing the floodlights and fencing on the Morocco and Spain border on the North Coast of Africa
 apni vaarshik report main mantralay ne likhaa he ki bhartiya kshetra main aatankiyon or apravasiyon kii ghuspaith ko rokane ke liye pakistan or bangladesh se lagati hui bharat kii 647 kilometre kii seemaa par flud lits lagaai gai hai
 After the matter came to light, the Home Secretary has sought a clarification from the officials and said that he would apologize if there was a mistake by the Ministry
 kendriya grih sachiv rajeev maharishi ne kaha ki koi zarurat nahin thi in tasveeron ke istemaal karne kii
 There are also many good pictures of our range
 unhone kaha ki ve pataa laga rahe hai ki ye tasviir kahaan se lee gayi or agar galat hui to maafi maang lenge
 The Home Secretary has also sought a clarification from the Border Security Force (BSF) on the matter
 darasal, bharat-pakistan seemaa kii tasviren aksar biguef hi muhaiyaa karwaati he
 To prevent incessant infiltration from Pakistan, India has put flood lights on its outskirts
 mantralay kii ore se in flud lits ke bare main 2016-17 kii vaarshik report main jaankaree di gai
 But the photographs used to give information about flood lights on the border are from the spain-morocco border

 5 staralagbhag 7 saal pehle sani deol kii ek film ko banane kii prakriya shuru hui jisamen ek se badhkar ek sitare jaise priti jinta, arshad varsi ,shreyas talapade, sanjay mishra ityadi ne ek-ek karke bhaag liya lekin film banate banate or final cat ke nikalne main 7 saal lag gaye
 In the past, Sunny Deol's films 'yamla Pagla Deewana Phir Se' and 'mohalla Assi' have beaten badly and now their film 'bhaiyaji Superhit' will get them a hit? Let us know how this film is finally in Neeraj Pathak's direction
 kahanefilm kii kahani varanasi ke rahane vaale dabang bhaiyaji (sani deol) kii he, jise apni patni sapana dube ( priti jinta ) se beintahaa mohabbat he
 But some such incidents happen due to which Sapna leaves home and Bhaiyaji gets upset
 patni ko ghar waapas laane ke liye vah tarah-tarah ke upaay sochate hai, jisamen film diarector goldi kapur (arshad varsi) film riter tarun porno ghosh (shreyas talapade) doctor gyaan prakaash buddhisagar (sanjay mishra) builder gupta (pankaj treepathi) or abhinetri mallika (amisha patel) kii entry hoti he
 Bhaiyaji wants to return his wife Sapna by making a film over his life
 vahiin duusari taraf bhaiyaji kaa dushman helicopter mishra (jayadeep ahlavat) he
 Which Bhaiyaji does not like at all and this enmity has been going on for many years
 ab kya bhaiyaji kii jindagi main sapana kii vaapasi hoti he or helicopter mishra se unki dushmani kaa anjaam kya hota he
 You have to watch the film to know all this
 kamazor kadiyanfilm kii kahani bahut hi kamjor he
 For this reason, the presence of so many good actors also seems quite dull
 kaha ja saktaa he ki is kahani ne sabhi actors kaa abhinay puri tareeke se duba diya he
 Any character is ever ready to do anything and the story appears helplessly to reach a conclusion in some way
 kaaphi dishaheen kahani he
 Although there is laughter at some places, but a good film continued to be made
 film kaa diarection kaaphi kamjor he or screenple ke saath saath cinemetography bhi dhili he
 The film's songs have not been a hit even before release and he also disappoints during filming
 unka aagaaj or anjaam donon feekaa he or climex to kaaphi bor karata he
 Why watch the film? Sunny Deol's rambunctious action, Arshad Warsi and Shreyas Talpade's comedy jugalbandi and Sanjay Mishra's few punches can entertain you
 yadi aap in sitaron ke diwane hai to ek baar jarur tri kar sakate hai
 Otherwise, wait till you come on TV
 box offisitani badi star cast ke saath film kaa bajet lagbhag 30 karod bataaya ja rahaa he
 It will be very interesting to see how this film performs at the box office

 The accused in the Samjhauta Express blast, Aseemanand, has described the news of Caravan magazine as false and artificial
 kaaravaan ne aseemanand ke saath baatcheet kaa hawala dete hue kaha tha ki samjhauta, ajmer, maalegaanv or makka masjid main hue dhamaakon kii manjuuri aresas ke sheersh netritv ne di thi
 After receiving this news, Aseemanand has written a letter to Caravan magazine on Thursday saying that he has not said any such thing
 unhone kaaravaan ke khilaaf mukadmaa karne kii chetavanee di he, haalanki aseemanand ne yah mana he ki vah kaaravaan kii reporter se mili the, lekin sirf saamaajik kaaryon ko lekar baatcheet kaa vah daawa kar rahe hai
 At the same time, Aseemanand's lawyer says that his client has not given any such interview
 is tepe kii sachai ko lekar aresas or bijepi ke sawaalon par kaaravaan ke kaaryakari sampadak vinod jose ne kaha he ki sachai ke liye agar court bhi janaa pade to vah iske liye taiyaar hai
 Despite the moderation in inflation in manufactured products, food and fuel inflation is likely to remain under pressure, RBI believes that the inflation for the next financial year will remain at the current level
 bhartiya rigerv bank (arabiai) ne maudrik niti kii mangalvaar ko jari madhya timahi samiksha main kaha ki kshetravaar str par maang or aapurti ke asantulan, vastuon ke prashasit mulyon main vruddhi or iske parinami prabhaavon ke maddenjar sakal mudrasphiti thodaa ghat bad ke saath maujuuda str par bani rah sakati he
 The central bank's review report said that in February 2013, inflation based on the wholesale price index of gross goods increased to 6
 84 par ho gai jo janvari main 6
 It was 6 percent
 prakatat: yah petroleum utpaadon ke prashasit mulyon main sanshodhan (vruddhi) kaa prabhaav lagata he
 At the same time, the central inflation (inflation of manufactured products) started in September 2012 in view of the decrease in the price of metals, textiles and rubber products continued and in February it was 3
 8 fisad par rahi
 However, the RBI said that retail inflation still remained in a worrying range, 10 in February 2013
 9 fisad ke str par rahi
 The central bank has said that inflationary expectations are also being impacted by the high price of food products, increased pressure on raising the minimum support price and the competition between wholesale and retail inflation
 arabiai ne sarkaar se krishi utpaadon ke nunatam samarthan mulya ko badhaane ke maamle main saavdhaanee baratane kaa suzav diya he kyonki iskaa sakal mudrasphiti par asar hota he
 In its mid-quarter review outlook, the RBI said that the inflation in manufactured products is coming down due to the reduction in the price of commodities globally and the ability of companies to increase prices due to reduced demand in the domestic market
 tippaniyan However, due to continuous increase in food inflation, wholesale price based gross inflation is above the ceiling and consumer price inflation is in double digits
 kendriya bank ne kaha ki kul milakar mudrasphiti kaa prabandhan jatil prakriya ban gaya he or aapurti paksh kii dikkaton ko dur karne kii aavashyaktaa jaahir hoti he
 The Reserve Bank of India (RBI) said in its mid-quarter Review of Monetary Policy on Tuesday that gross inflation moderated slightly at current levels in view of demand-supply imbalance at the sector level, increase in administered prices of commodities and its consequent effects
 Can persist
 kendriya bank kii samiksha rapat main kaha gaya he ki farvari 2013 main sakal vastuon ke thok mulya suchakank par aadhaarit mudrasphiti bad kar 6
 84, which turned out to be 6 in January
 6 fisad thi
 Apparently this seems to be the effect of the revision (increase) in administered prices of petroleum products
 saath hi dhaatu, kapadaa or rabar utpaadon kii keemat main kami ke maddenjar sitambar 2012 main shuru hui kendriya mudrasphiti (vinirmit utpaadon kii mudrasphiti) main kami jari rahi or farvari main yah 3
 Remained at 8 percent

 It was at the level of 9 percent

 The RBI has suggested the government to be cautious in raising the minimum support price for agricultural products as it has an impact on gross inflation
 arabiai ne madhya timahi samiksha ke drushtikon main kaha ki vaishvik str par jinson kii keemat main kami or gharelu bazaar main maang kam hone ke kaaran companiyon kii keemat badhaane kii kshamta kam hone ke kaaran vinirmit utpaadon kii mudrasphiti kam ho rahi he

 aaj tak ke vishesh kaarykram sidhi baat main dilli kii mukhyamantri shila dikshit ne india today group ke sampadakeey nideshak prabhu chawla se jagadish titalar maamle se lekar raajnneeti or congress party ke bare main apni bebaak raay di
 Significantly, Sheila Dixit has become the Chief Minister of Delhi for the third time in a row and is campaigning for the Congress outside Delhi in view of the Lok Sabha elections
 is par shila kaa kahana he ki uttar pradesh se unka rishta he, wo uttar pradesh kii bahu hai isliye vahaan chunaav prachaar ke liye ja rahi hai
 Regarding the withdrawal of tickets from Jagdish Tytler, Sheila said that Tytler was given a unanimous ticket and the ticket was also withdrawn unanimously
 unhone kaha ki titalar maamle ko jaanboojhkar mudda banaaya gaya
 Sheila said that the Akali Dal and the BJP knew that the Congress was doing well in Punjab, so they made Tytler's case an issue
 unhone congress dwaara titalar se tikat waapas lene ke faisle ko sahi tehraate hue kaha ki har party ke liye chunavi hit bhi ahm hote hai
 He said that in this case the party did not take any decision fearfully but heard the voice of the public
 jab unase poocha gaya ki kya juuta prakaran kii vajah se hi titalar ko hataanaa padaa to unhone kaha ki usee prakaran ne janata ke gusse ko bhadakaayaa
 He also said that this method of protest by the public is wrong
 jab unase poocha gaya ki jis tarah netaaon par juute or chappal phenke ja rahe hai usase aisa nahin lagata ki netaa or janata ke bich kii duuri bad rahi he, to shila ne kaha ki aisa nahin he
 This time many rich ummidwar are also in the fray in the Lok Sabha elections
 congress main bhi kai karodpati ummidavaar shaamil hai
 On this, Sheila Dixit says that Congress is not a party of the rich, but yes some people with money have definitely got the taste of politics
 raajnneeti main apradhi kism ke logon ke badhati taadaad par shila ne kaha ki isse bhartiya raajnneeti ko nuksaan ho rahaa he or wo iske bilkul khilaaf hai
 He even said that candidates who have a bad image should also avoid giving tickets
 jab unase poocha gaya ki bhavishya main congress kii ore se gandhi parivaar ke kisi sadsy ko chhodkar or kisi ke pradhanmantri banane kii ummid he ki nahin, to shila ne kaha ki koi nahin jaanata tha ki manmohan singh pradhanmantri banenge
 But Sonia Gandhi made Manmohan Singh the Prime Minister
 isliye bhavishya main kya hoga ye kaha nahin ja saktaa or party kii ore se koi bhi piem ban saktaa he
